# API: DefaultApi

All URIs are relative to *https://s3.amazonaws.com/*

<a name="markdown-header-op-DefaultApi-abort_multipart_upload"></a>

## operation: **abort_multipart_upload**


<p>Aborts a multipart upload.</p> <p>To verify that all parts have been removed, so you don't get charged for the part storage, you should call the List Parts operation and ensure the parts list is empty.</p><p>http://docs.amazonwebservices.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/mpUploadAbort.html</p>


### Example
```abap
*** method DefaultApi->abort_multipart_upload example

  constants:
    gcc_basepath type string value 'https://s3.amazonaws.com/'.
    
  data:  
    gvi_code type /blck/as3_int,
    gvs_msg  type /blck/as3_string.
    
*** create variables for input and output as needed
*   for parameter i_body:
*   a reference to model type /BLCK/AS3_ABORTMULTIPAR2
    data gm_body type /BLCK/AS3_ABORTMULTIPAR2.
*   for parameter i_bucket:
*   a simple ABAP primitive of type /BLCK/AS3_STRING
    data gvs_bucket type /BLCK/AS3_STRING.
*   for parameter i_key:
*   a simple ABAP primitive of type /BLCK/AS3_STRING
    data gvs_key type /BLCK/AS3_STRING.
*   for parameter i_x_amz_security_token:
*   a simple ABAP primitive of type /BLCK/AS3_STRING
    data gvs_x_amz_security_token type /BLCK/AS3_STRING.
*   when the result of the call is HTTP Code: 200 we expect type /BLCK/AS3_ABORTMULTIPART
```

<a name="markdown-header-op-DefaultApi-create_multipart_upload"></a>

## operation: **create_multipart_upload**


<p>Initiates a multipart upload and returns an upload ID.</p> <p> <b>Note:</b> After you initiate multipart upload and upload one or more parts, you must either complete or abort multipart upload in order to stop getting charged for storage of the uploaded parts. Only after you either complete or abort multipart upload, Amazon S3 frees up the parts storage and stops charging you for the parts storage.</p><p>http://docs.amazonwebservices.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/mpUploadInitiate.html</p>

## operation: **delete_object**


Removes the null version (if there is one) of an object and inserts a delete marker, which becomes the latest version of the object. If there isn't a null version, Amazon S3 does not remove any objects.<p>http://docs.amazonwebservices.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/RESTObjectDELETE.html</p>

To use HEAD, you must have READ access to the object.<p>http://docs.amazonwebservices.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/RESTObjectHEAD.html</p>

<a name="markdown-header-op-DefaultApi-put_bucket_request_payment"></a>

## operation: **put_bucket_request_payment**


Sets the request payment configuration for a bucket. By default, the bucket owner pays for downloads from the bucket. This configuration parameter enables the bucket owner (only) to specify that the person requesting the download will be charged for the download. Documentation on requester pays buckets can be found at http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/RequesterPaysBuckets.html<p>http://docs.amazonwebservices.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/RESTrequestPaymentPUT.html</p>

<a name="markdown-header-op-DefaultApi-put_object_lock_configuration"></a>

## operation: **put_object_lock_configuration**


Places an Object Lock configuration on the specified bucket. The rule specified in the Object Lock configuration will be applied by default to every new object placed in the specified bucket.


### Example
```abap
*** method DefaultApi->put_object_lock_configuration example

  constants:
    gcc_basepath type string value 'https://s3.amazonaws.com/'.
```

<a name="markdown-header-op-DefaultApi-select_object_content"></a>

## operation: **select_object_content**


This operation filters the contents of an Amazon S3 object based on a simple Structured Query Language (SQL) statement. In the request, along with the SQL expression, you must also specify a data serialization format (JSON or CSV) of the object. Amazon S3 uses this to parse object data into records, and returns only records that match the specified SQL expression. You must also specify the data serialization format for the response.

<a name="markdown-header-op-DefaultApi-upload_part"></a>

## operation: **upload_part**


<p>Uploads a part in a multipart upload.</p> <p> <b>Note:</b> After you initiate multipart upload and upload one or more parts, you must either complete or abort multipart upload in order to stop getting charged for storage of the uploaded parts. Only after you either complete or abort multipart upload, Amazon S3 frees up the parts storage and stops charging you for the parts storage.</p><p>http://docs.amazonwebservices.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/mpUploadUploadPart.html</p>

<a name="markdown-header-model-abortincomplet"></a> 

# Model: AbortIncompleteMultipartUpload



### Example
```abap
*** model abortincomplet example
*** Specifies  the  days  since the initiation of an Incomplete Multipart Upload
*** that  Lifecycle  will  wait  before  permanently  removing  all parts of the
*** upload.

* create our variables..
```

```abap
*** transition  to  the  STANDARD_IA, ONEZONE_IA, INTELLIGENT_TIERING or GLACIER

*** suspended),  you  can  set  this action to request that Amazon S3 transition
*** noncurrent    object    versions    to    the    STANDARD_IA,    ONEZONE_IA,
*** INTELLIGENT_TIERING  or  GLACIER  storage  class at a specific period in the
*** object&#x27;s lifetime.
```

```abap
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_bucketlocation-ap_south_1.

    when /blck/as3_const=>me_bucketlocation-ap_southeast_1.
*     do something specific to ap_southeast_1 case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_bucketlocation-ap_southeast_2.
*     do something specific to ap_southeast_2 case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_bucketlocation-ap_northeast_1.
*     do something specific to ap_northeast_1 case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_bucketlocation-sa_east_1.
*     do something specific to sa_east_1 case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_bucketlocation-cn_north_1.
*     do something specific to cn_north_1 case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_bucketlocation-eu_central_1.
*     do something specific to eu_central_1 case..
  endcase.


```

```abap
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3reducedredundancylostob.
*     do something specific to s3reducedredundancylostob case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3_object_created_.
*     do something specific to s3_object_created_ case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3_object_created_put.
*     do something specific to s3_object_created_put case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3_object_created_post.
*     do something specific to s3_object_created_post case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3_object_created_copy.
*     do something specific to s3_object_created_copy case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3objectcreatedcompletemu.
*     do something specific to s3objectcreatedcompletemu case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3_object_removed_.
*     do something specific to s3_object_removed_ case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3_object_removed_delete.
*     do something specific to s3_object_removed_delete case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3objectremoveddeletemark.
*     do something specific to s3objectremoveddeletemark case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3_object_restore_post.
*     do something specific to s3_object_restore_post case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_event-s3objectrestorecompleted.
*     do something specific to s3objectrestorecompleted case..
  endcase.
```

<a name="markdown-header-enum-compressiontyp"></a> 

# Enum: CompressionType



### Example
```abap
*** model compressiontyp example

* create our variables..
    data gv_compressiontyp type /blck/as3_compressiontyp.
    
* set the enum value we want
    gv_compressiontyp = /blck/as3_const=>me_compressiontyp-none.
    
* pass the enum value to the example API via method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>set_compressiontyp_state(
      exporting
        i_compressiontyp = gv_compressiontyp ).
    		
    clear gv_compressiontyp.
    
* fetch result from example API method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>get_compressiontyp_state(
      exporting
        i_id = 1
      importing
        e_200 = gv_compressiontyp ).
    	
* we can handle the result with either "if" with individual cases
* or use a case clause to handle all scenarios:
  case gv_compressiontyp.
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_compressiontyp-none.
*     do something specific to none case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_compressiontyp-gzip.
*     do something specific to gzip case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_compressiontyp-bzip2.
*     do something specific to bzip2 case..
  endcase.


```

## Enum Values

Name | Value | Constant
------------ | ------------- | -------------
**none** | NONE | `/blck/as3_const=>me_compressiontyp-none`
**gzip** | GZIP | `/blck/as3_const=>me_compressiontyp-gzip`
**bzip2** | BZIP2 | `/blck/as3_const=>me_compressiontyp-bzip2`

# Model: DeletedObject



### Example
```abap
*** model deleted_object example

* create our variables..
    data gr_deleted_object type /blck/as3_deleted_object.
    
* fill model with data as appropriate..
    gr_deleted_object-key = l_key. " (type /BLCK/AS3_OBJECT_KEY)
    gr_deleted_object-version_id = l_version_id. " (type /BLCK/AS3_OBJECTVERSIONI)
    gr_deleted_object-delete_marker = l_delete_marker. " (type /BLCK/AS3_DELETE_MARKER)
    gr_deleted_object-delete_marker_version_id = l_delete_marker_version_id. " (type /BLCK/AS3_DELETEMARKERVE)
    
* pass to example API method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>update_deleted_object(
      exporting
        i_deleted_object = gr_deleted_object ).
    		
    clear gr_deleted_object.
    
* fetch model data from example API method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>get_deleted_object(
      exporting
        i_id = 1
      importing 
        e_200 = gr_deleted_object ).
    		
    write: gr_deleted_object-key. " (type /BLCK/AS3_OBJECT_KEY)
    write: gr_deleted_object-version_id. " (type /BLCK/AS3_OBJECTVERSIONI)
    write: gr_deleted_object-delete_marker. " (type /BLCK/AS3_DELETE_MARKER)
    write: gr_deleted_object-delete_marker_version_id. " (type /BLCK/AS3_DELETEMARKERVE)

```

## Properties

Name | Type | Description
------------ | ------------- | -------------
**key** | `/BLCK/AS3_OBJECT_KEY` (**[ObjectKey](#markdown-header-model-object_key)**) | 
**version_id** | `/BLCK/AS3_OBJECTVERSIONI` (**[ObjectVersionId](#markdown-header-model-objectversioni)**) | 
**delete_marker** | `/BLCK/AS3_DELETE_MARKER` (**[DeleteMarker](#markdown-header-model-delete_marker)**) | 
**delete_marker_version_id** | `/BLCK/AS3_DELETEMARKERVE` (**[DeleteMarkerVersionId](#markdown-header-model-deletemarkerve)**) |

<a name="markdown-header-enum-deletemarkerr2"></a> 

# Enum: DeleteMarkerReplicationStatus



### Example
```abap
*** model deletemarkerr2 example

* create our variables..
    data gv_deletemarkerr2 type /blck/as3_deletemarkerr2.
    
* set the enum value we want
    gv_deletemarkerr2 = /blck/as3_const=>me_deletemarkerr2-enabled.
    
* pass the enum value to the example API via method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>set_deletemarkerr2_state(
      exporting
        i_deletemarkerr2 = gv_deletemarkerr2 ).
    		
    clear gv_deletemarkerr2.
    
* fetch result from example API method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>get_deletemarkerr2_state(
      exporting
        i_id = 1
      importing
        e_200 = gv_deletemarkerr2 ).
    	
* we can handle the result with either "if" with individual cases
* or use a case clause to handle all scenarios:
  case gv_deletemarkerr2.
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_deletemarkerr2-enabled.
*     do something specific to enabled case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_deletemarkerr2-disabled.
*     do something specific to disabled case..
  endcase.


```

## Enum Values

Name | Value | Constant
------------ | ------------- | -------------
**enabled** | Enabled | `/blck/as3_const=>me_deletemarkerr2-enabled`
**disabled** | Disabled | `/blck/as3_const=>me_deletemarkerr2-disabled`

<a name="markdown-header-model-encryptionconf"></a> 

# Model: EncryptionConfiguration



### Example
```abap
*** model encryptionconf example
*** A  container  for  information  about the encryption-based configuration for
*** replicas.

* create our variables..
    data gr_encryptionconf type /blck/as3_encryptionconf.
    
* fill model with data as appropriate..
```

<a name="markdown-header-enum-encoding_type"></a> 

# Enum: EncodingType



### Example
```abap
*** model encoding_type example
*** Requests  Amazon  S3 to encode the object keys in the response and specifies
*** the encoding method to use. An object key may contain any Unicode character;
*** however,  XML  1.0  parser  cannot parse some characters, such as characters
*** with  an  ASCII value from 0 to 10. For characters that are not supported in
*** XML  1.0,  you  can  add this parameter to request that Amazon S3 encode the
*** keys in the response.

* create our variables..
    data gv_encoding_type type /blck/as3_encoding_type.
    
* set the enum value we want
```

# Enum: InventoryFormat



### Example
```abap
*** model inventoryforma example

* create our variables..
    data gv_inventoryforma type /blck/as3_inventoryforma.
    
* set the enum value we want
    gv_inventoryforma = /blck/as3_const=>me_inventoryforma-csv.
    
* pass the enum value to the example API via method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>set_inventoryforma_state(
      exporting
        i_inventoryforma = gv_inventoryforma ).
    		
    clear gv_inventoryforma.
    
* fetch result from example API method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>get_inventoryforma_state(
      exporting
        i_id = 1
      importing
        e_200 = gv_inventoryforma ).
    	
* we can handle the result with either "if" with individual cases
* or use a case clause to handle all scenarios:
  case gv_inventoryforma.
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_inventoryforma-csv.
*     do something specific to csv case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_inventoryforma-orc.
*     do something specific to orc case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_inventoryforma-parquet.
*     do something specific to parquet case..
  endcase.


```

```abap
    write: gr_publicaccessbl-ignore_public_acls. " (type /BLCK/AS3_SETTING)
    write: gr_publicaccessbl-block_public_policy. " (type /BLCK/AS3_SETTING)
    write: gr_publicaccessbl-restrict_public_buckets. " (type /BLCK/AS3_SETTING)
```

<a name="markdown-header-enum-tier"></a> 

# Enum: Tier



### Example
```abap
*** model tier example

* create our variables..
    data gv_tier type /blck/as3_tier.
    
* set the enum value we want
    gv_tier = /blck/as3_const=>me_tier-standard.
    
* pass the enum value to the example API via method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>set_tier_state(
      exporting
        i_tier = gv_tier ).
    		
    clear gv_tier.
    
* fetch result from example API method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>get_tier_state(
      exporting
        i_id = 1
      importing
        e_200 = gv_tier ).
    	
* we can handle the result with either "if" with individual cases
* or use a case clause to handle all scenarios:
  case gv_tier.
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_tier-standard.
*     do something specific to standard case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_tier-bulk.
*     do something specific to bulk case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_tier-expedited.
*     do something specific to expedited case..
  endcase.


```

## Enum Values

Name | Value | Constant
------------ | ------------- | -------------
**standard** | Standard | `/blck/as3_const=>me_tier-standard`
**bulk** | Bulk | `/blck/as3_const=>me_tier-bulk`
**expedited** | Expedited | `/blck/as3_const=>me_tier-expedited`

```abap
* or use a case clause to handle all scenarios:
  case gv_objectstoragec.
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_objectstoragec-standard.
*     do something specific to standard case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_objectstoragec-reduced_redundancy.
*     do something specific to reduced_redundancy case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_objectstoragec-glacier.
*     do something specific to glacier case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_objectstoragec-standard_ia.
*     do something specific to standard_ia case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_objectstoragec-onezone_ia.
*     do something specific to onezone_ia case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_objectstoragec-intelligent_tiering.
*     do something specific to intelligent_tiering case..
  endcase.


```

# Enum: ObjectLockMode



### Example
```abap
*** model objectlockmode example

* create our variables..
    data gv_objectlockmode type /blck/as3_objectlockmode.
    
* set the enum value we want
    gv_objectlockmode = /blck/as3_const=>me_objectlockmode-governance.
    
* pass the enum value to the example API via method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>set_objectlockmode_state(
      exporting
        i_objectlockmode = gv_objectlockmode ).
    		
    clear gv_objectlockmode.
    
* fetch result from example API method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>get_objectlockmode_state(
      exporting
        i_id = 1
      importing
        e_200 = gv_objectlockmode ).
    	
* we can handle the result with either "if" with individual cases
* or use a case clause to handle all scenarios:
  case gv_objectlockmode.
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_objectlockmode-governance.
*     do something specific to governance case..
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_objectlockmode-compliance.
*     do something specific to compliance case..
  endcase.


```

# Model: SelectObjectContentRequest



### Example
```abap
*** model selectobjectco example
*** Request  to  filter  the  contents  of an Amazon S3 object based on a simple
*** Structured  Query  Language  (SQL) statement. In the request, along with the
*** SQL  expression,  you must specify a data serialization format (JSON or CSV)
*** of  the  object.  Amazon  S3 uses this to parse object data into records. It
*** returns  only records that match the specified SQL expression. You must also
*** specify   the   data   serialization  format  for  the  response.  For  more
*** information,                              see                             &lt;a
*** href&#x3D;\&quot;http://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/API/RESTObjectSELECTContent.html\&quot;&gt;S3Select
*** API Documentation&lt;/a&gt;.

* create our variables..
    data gr_selectobjectco type /blck/as3_selectobjectco.
    
* fill model with data as appropriate..
    gr_selectobjectco-expression = l_expression. " (type /BLCK/AS3_EXPRESSION)
    gr_selectobjectco-expression_type = /blck/as3_const=>me_expressiontype-sql. " (enum /BLCK/AS3_EXPRESSIONTYPE)
    gr_selectobjectco-request_progress = l_request_progress. " (type /BLCK/AS3_REQUESTPROGRES)
    gr_selectobjectco-input_serialization = l_input_serialization. " (type /BLCK/AS3_INPUTSERIALIZA)
    gr_selectobjectco-output_serialization = l_output_serialization. " (type /BLCK/AS3_OUTPUTSERIALIZ)
    
* pass to example API method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>update_selectobjectco(
      exporting
        i_selectobjectco = gr_selectobjectco ).
    		
    clear gr_selectobjectco.
    
* fetch model data from example API method
    /blck/cl_example_api=>get_selectobjectco(
      exporting
        i_id = 1
      importing 
        e_200 = gr_selectobjectco ).
    		
    write: gr_selectobjectco-expression. " (type /BLCK/AS3_EXPRESSION)
    write: gr_selectobjectco-expression_type. " (type /BLCK/AS3_EXPRESSIONTYPE)
    write: gr_selectobjectco-request_progress. " (type /BLCK/AS3_REQUESTPROGRES)
    write: gr_selectobjectco-input_serialization. " (type /BLCK/AS3_INPUTSERIALIZA)
    write: gr_selectobjectco-output_serialization. " (type /BLCK/AS3_OUTPUTSERIALIZ)
```

```abap
* or use a case clause to handle all scenarios:
  case gv_taggingdirecti.
    when /blck/as3_const=>me_taggingdirecti-copy.
```
